<p><b>Raphaël Xavier Varane</b> (born 25 April 1993) is a French professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre-back" title="Defender (association football)">centre-back</a> for Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> and the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France national team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_madrid_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_madrid-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Varane previously played for French club <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">Lens</a> and, ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_in_French_football" title="201011 in French football">201011 season</a>, began training with the senior team and appeared on the bench in several league matches. Varane made his professional debut in 2010 aged 17, in a league match against <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_debut_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_debut-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> After one season with the French club, and as a professional footballer, Varane joined Real Madrid in the summer of 2011.
</p><p>Since joining Real Madrid, Varane has made over 300 appearances for the club and has won 18 major honours, including three <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> titles, one <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> title, four <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> titles and four <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="FIFA Club World Cup">FIFA Club World Cup</a> titles.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> At only 24 years of age, Varane won the UEFA Champions League for the third time, making him the youngest defender ever to have won the trophy three times, beating <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Maldini" title="Paolo Maldini">Paolo Maldini</a> who was 26 when he won his third.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Varane was a <a href="/wiki/France_national_youth_football_team" title="France national youth football team">France youth international</a>, having earned caps at <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-18_football_team" title="France national under-18 football team">under-18</a>, <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-20_football_team" title="France national under-20 football team">under-20</a> and <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-21_football_team" title="France national under-21 football team">under-21</a> level. He made his full international debut in March 2013 and represented the country at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>, a tournament where he was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Best_Young_Player_Award" title="FIFA World Cup awards">Best Young Player</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
He won the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in which he played every minute of every game.
</p><p>Varane has been described by Lens youth coach <a href="/wiki/Eric_Assadourian" class="mw-redirect" title="Eric Assadourian">Eric Assadourian</a> as a "truly first class player" who is "comfortable on both the tactical and technical level".<sup id="cite_ref-lensois_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lensois-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He was called the best defender in the world by <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Hierro" title="Fernando Hierro">Fernando Hierro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> in 2013 and 2014, respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-goal1_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal1-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-goal2_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal2-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Varane was born in the city of <a href="/wiki/Lille" title="Lille">Lille</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Nord-Pas-de-Calais" title="Nord-Pas-de-Calais">Nord-Pas-de-Calais</a> <a href="/wiki/Regions_of_France" title="Regions of France">region</a>. He is of <a href="/wiki/Martinique" title="Martinique">Martiniquais</a> heritage through his father, Gaston, who is originally from <a href="/wiki/Le_Morne-Rouge" title="Le Morne-Rouge">Le Morne-Rouge</a>, while his mother, Annie, was raised in <a href="/wiki/Saint-Amand-les-Eaux" title="Saint-Amand-les-Eaux">Saint-Amand-les-Eaux</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_antilles_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_antilles-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Varane began his football career in the <a href="/wiki/Arrondissement_of_Lille" title="Arrondissement of Lille">Arrondissement of Lille</a> playing for local club AS Hellemmes at the age of seven.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> After spending two years at the club, in July 2002, he joined professional club <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">RC Lens</a>, despite some interest from <a href="/wiki/Derby_du_Nord" title="Derby du Nord">Derby du Nord</a> rivals and hometown club <a href="/wiki/Lille_OSC" title="Lille OSC">Lille OSC</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_career_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_career-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Similar to the development of the club's previous prized assets such as <a href="/wiki/Ga%C3%ABl_Kakuta" title="Gaël Kakuta">Gaël Kakuta</a> and <a href="/wiki/Timoth%C3%A9e_Kolodziejczak" title="Timothée Kolodziejczak">Timothée Kolodziejczak</a>, Varane spent time at the Centre de Préformation de Football in nearby <a href="/wiki/Li%C3%A9vin" title="Liévin">Liévin</a>, a training center exclusively for players brought up in the <a href="/wiki/Nord-Pas-de-Calais" title="Nord-Pas-de-Calais">Nord-Pas-de-Calais</a> <a href="/wiki/Regions_of_France" title="Regions of France">region</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_antilles_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_antilles-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He spent two years at the center training there during the weekdays and playing with Lens on the weekends.
</p><p>After returning full-time to Lens, Varane quickly ascended up the club's youth ranks. In the 200809 season, alongside teammates <a href="/wiki/Thorgan_Hazard" title="Thorgan Hazard">Thorgan Hazard</a> and <a href="/wiki/Geoffrey_Kondogbia" title="Geoffrey Kondogbia">Geoffrey Kondogbia</a>, he played on the club's under-16 team that won the <i>Championnat National des 16 ans</i>. In the following season, Varane was promoted to the club's under-19 team, despite being two years younger than several of his teammates. Ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_in_French_football" title="201011 in French football">201011 season</a>, Varane signed his first professional contract.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He was, subsequently, promoted to the club's reserve team in the <a href="/wiki/Championnat_de_France_amateur" class="mw-redirect" title="Championnat de France amateur">Championnat de France amateur</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Varane made his amateur debut in the club's opening league match of the campaign in a 20 victory over <a href="/wiki/JA_Drancy" title="JA Drancy">Drancy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> He appeared as a starter in the club's next nine matches with the team losing only one of them.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lens">Lens</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Lens">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In late October of the campaign, Varane was called up to the senior team by manager <a href="/wiki/Jean-Guy_Wallemme" title="Jean-Guy Wallemme">Jean-Guy Wallemme</a> to train ahead of the club's match against <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a> on 6 November. He trained with the team for the entire week and, due to an injury to <a href="/wiki/Defender_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Defender (football)">centre-back</a> <a href="/wiki/Alaeddine_Yahia" title="Alaeddine Yahia">Alaeddine Yahia</a>, Varane was, surprisingly, named to the starting lineup.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> In the match, he played the full 90 minutes in a 20 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_debut_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_debut-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> The victory was only the club's third <a href="/wiki/Clean_sheet" class="mw-redirect" title="Clean sheet">clean sheet</a> of the season. Varane was praised by teammates, most notably <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> <a href="/wiki/Adil_Hermach" title="Adil Hermach">Adil Hermach</a>, defending partner <a href="/wiki/Eric_Chelle" class="mw-redirect" title="Eric Chelle">Eric Chelle</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Striker_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Striker (association football)">striker</a> <a href="/wiki/David_Pollet" title="David Pollet">David Pollet</a>, as well as by the local media and coach Wallemme.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> In the next two matches, Varane, alongside several other youth players, sat on the bench as Lens faced two tough teams in <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a> and <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Lyon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He returned to the starting lineup on 30 November in a 41 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Stade_Brestois_29" title="Stade Brestois 29">Brest</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Despite the firing of Wallemme following the Brest match, Varane remained a starter in the team under new manager <a href="/wiki/L%C3%A1szl%C3%B3_B%C3%B6l%C3%B6ni" title="László Bölöni">László Bölöni</a>. In December, with both Chelle and Yahia returning to action, Varane was placed in the defensive midfielder role in the team's match against <a href="/wiki/FC_Girondins_de_Bordeaux" title="FC Girondins de Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a>. In the match, he acted as a roving third centre-back and made a blocked save in the 84th minute on a close range shot by <a href="/wiki/Yoan_Gouffran" title="Yoan Gouffran">Yoan Gouffran</a> to preserve a 21 lead.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> However, in the latter stages of the match, Bordeaux equalized to draw the match at 22.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In early 2011, Varane was the subject of transfer speculation with the player being linked to several clubs.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> In an effort to quell the interest, on 3 February 2011, he signed a two-year contract extension with Lens until 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 8 May, Varane scored his first professional goal in a 11 draw with <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">Caen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> In the team's following match against <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>, he scored the equalizing goal in another 11 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Despite the goal, the stalemate condemned Lens to relegation back to Ligue 2 after two seasons in the top division.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> On 21 May, Varane <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captained</a> Lens in its 10 defeat to <a href="/wiki/AC_Arles-Avignon" title="AC Arles-Avignon">Arles-Avignon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Madrid">Real Madrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Real Madrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9312_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201112_season">201112 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 201112 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane_in_Real_Madrid.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane_in_Real_Madrid.jpg/170px-Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane_in_Real_Madrid.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="328" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane_in_Real_Madrid.jpg/255px-Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane_in_Real_Madrid.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/86/Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane_in_Real_Madrid.jpg 2x" data-file-width="339" data-file-height="655" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane_in_Real_Madrid.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Varane training with <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>On 22 June 2011, Lens president <a href="/wiki/Gervais_Martel" title="Gervais Martel">Gervais Martel</a> confirmed to a group of supporters at a club meeting that Varane would be joining Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> stating, "He will play for Real Madrid under the guidance of <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a>."<sup id="cite_ref-varane_madrid_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_madrid-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Varane had previously visited Real Madrid's club facilities and also met with club advisor and compatriot <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_madrid_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_madrid-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> On 27 June, the move was confirmed by Real Madrid after Varane successfully passed his medical. Varane signed a six-year contract with the club and the transfer fee is purported to be in the range of 10&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Varane was assigned the number 19 shirt and made his club debut for Real Madrid in the club's opening pre-season fixture against American outfit <a href="/wiki/LA_Galaxy" title="LA Galaxy">Los Angeles Galaxy</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2011_World_Football_Challenge" title="2011 World Football Challenge">2011 World Football Challenge</a>. He appeared as a half-time substitute as Real Madrid cruised to a 41 win.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Varane made his first start for the club four days later in a 30 win over Mexican club <a href="/wiki/C.D._Guadalajara" title="C.D. Guadalajara">Guadalajara</a>. He finished the pre-season campaign appearing in seven of the eight pre-season matches Real Madrid contested.
</p><p>Varane made his competitive debut for Real Madrid on 21 September in the team's league match against <a href="/wiki/Racing_de_Santander" title="Racing de Santander">Racing de Santander</a>. He started the match at centre-back alongside <a href="/wiki/Ricardo_Carvalho" title="Ricardo Carvalho">Ricardo Carvalho</a> as the match ended 00.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> In the team's next league match three days later against <a href="/wiki/Rayo_Vallecano" title="Rayo Vallecano">Rayo Vallecano</a>, Varane started and scored his first goal for the club after a flying back-heel shot following a <a href="/wiki/Mesut_%C3%96zil" title="Mesut Özil">Mesut Özil</a> corner. Real Madrid won the match 62. Varane's goal made him the youngest foreign player at 18 years and 152 days to score a goal in a competitive match for Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> On 27 September, he made his <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> debut in a 30 group stage win over Dutch club <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Two months later, Varane made his second Champions League appearance against Croatian club <a href="/wiki/GNK_Dinamo_Zagreb" title="GNK Dinamo Zagreb">Dinamo Zagreb</a>. In the match, Varane started and assisted on the team's fifth goal, scored by <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Callej%C3%B3n" title="José Callejón">José Callejón</a>, in a 62 win. The victory ensured Real Madrid first place in its group.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9313_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201213_season">201213 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 201213 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_La_Liga" title="201213 La Liga">201213 season</a>, Varane switched to the number 2 shirt. After failing to appear in Real Madrid's first four league matches, he made his season debut on 18 September in the club's opening UEFA Champions League group stage match against English club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>. Varane started and played the entire match as Real Madrid won 32.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 30 January 2013, Varane made his <i><a href="/wiki/El_Cl%C3%A1sico" title="El Clásico">El Clásico</a></i> debut against <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Copa_del_Rey" title="201213 Copa del Rey">201213 Copa del Rey</a>. He stopped a group of dangerous attempts from Barcelona, including a shot from <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a> that he cleared from the goal line. He capped his performance with a headed goal in the game, which ended 11. He also became the second-youngest foreign player to score for Real Madrid in a Clásico match. In the return leg at the <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a> on 26 February 2013, Varane scored Madrid's third goal in a 31 away win with a header from a corner kick by Mesut Özil. Varane gained praise from former World Cup winner <a href="/wiki/Bixente_Lizarazu" title="Bixente Lizarazu">Bixente Lizarazu</a> after his performances against Barcelona and <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>. He said, "We are talking about a kid at Real Madrid who has unseated <a href="/wiki/Pepe_(footballer_born_1983)" class="mw-redirect" title="Pepe (footballer born 1983)">Pepe</a>, and Pepe, with all his stuff, is still a great centre-half. His performance against Manchester United and Barcelona was extraordinary". Varane continued to impress in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201213 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> quarter final first leg against <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K._(football)" title="Galatasaray S.K. (football)">Galatasaray</a>, where he helped Madrid keep a <a href="/wiki/Clean_sheet" class="mw-redirect" title="Clean sheet">clean sheet</a> in a 30 triumph. All of his 27 passes found his teammates without any interception, and all of his tackles succeeded, with most on <a href="/wiki/Didier_Drogba" title="Didier Drogba">Didier Drogba</a>.
</p><p>In April 2013, Varane was named by <a href="/wiki/Marca_(newspaper)" title="Marca (newspaper)"><i>Marca</i></a> readers as a member of the "Best foreign eleven in <a href="/wiki/History_of_Real_Madrid_CF" title="History of Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid's history</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> On 14 May 2013, Varane successfully underwent an operation on his right knee after an injury he had picked up during his last 201213 league match against <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a>.
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201314_season">201314 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 201314 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Varane came on as an injury-time substitute for <a href="/wiki/Karim_Benzema" title="Karim Benzema">Karim Benzema</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2014_Copa_del_Rey_Final" title="2014 Copa del Rey Final">2014 Copa del Rey Final</a> which Real Madrid won 21 against Barcelona on 16 April.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He played all 120 minutes of Real Madrid's 41 win over <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2014 UEFA Champions League Final">2014 UEFA Champions League Final</a>, in place of the more experienced Pepe. In added time at the end of extra time, after <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> scored the last goal, Varane kicked the ball towards Atlético manager <a href="/wiki/Diego_Simeone" title="Diego Simeone">Diego Simeone</a>, causing him to run onto the pitch in anger. Simeone was sent to the stands and Varane booked for the incident. After the game, Atlético captain <a href="/wiki/Gabi_(footballer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Gabi (footballer)">Gabi</a> excused Varane due to his youth, while Simeone himself said, "I also made a mistake with my reaction. He's a young guy with a bright future."<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201415_season">201415 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 201415 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 18 September 2014, Varane signed a new six-year contract that will keep him at Real Madrid until 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201516_season">201516 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 201516 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Varane was a part-time starter when the team won the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201516 UEFA Champions League">201516 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201617_season">201617 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 201617 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite having a few injuries during the season, he made 23 appearances, when Madrid won the 201617 La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> He was starting in the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2017 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a> when Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201617 UEFA Champions League">201617 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201718_season">201718 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 201718 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Liver-RM_(8)_cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Liver-RM_%288%29_cropped%29.jpg/170px-Liver-RM_%288%29_cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="219" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Liver-RM_%288%29_cropped%29.jpg/255px-Liver-RM_%288%29_cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Liver-RM_%288%29_cropped%29.jpg/340px-Liver-RM_%288%29_cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="573" data-file-height="739" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Liver-RM_(8)_cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Varane after winning the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201718 UEFA Champions League">201718 UEFA Champions League</a> with Real Madrid</div></div></div>
<p>Varane's contract was extended until 2022 on 27 September 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201718 UEFA Champions League">201718 UEFA Champions League</a>, he made eleven appearances, when Madrid won their third consecutive and 13th overall Champions League title.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Following his club and international performances throughout the year, he was included in the 30-man shortlist for the <a href="/wiki/2018_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2018 Ballon d&#39;Or">2018 Ballon d'Or</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> finishing in seventh place in the final ranking.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> He was also placed ninth in <a href="/wiki/The_Best_FIFA_Football_Awards_2018" title="The Best FIFA Football Awards 2018">The Best FIFA Men's Player</a> behind <a href="/wiki/Kevin_De_Bruyne" title="Kevin De Bruyne">Kevin De Bruyne</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Voting_Results_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Voting_Results-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> and was elected as the starting centre-back for both the 2018 <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#Awards" title="FIFPro">FIFPro Men's World11</a><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year#Team_of_the_Year_2018" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-team2018_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-team2018-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201819_season">201819 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 201819 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>During the season, he made 43 appearances, while winning the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA Club World Cup">2018 FIFA Club World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201920_season">201920 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 201920 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>He was a regular starter during the league season, as Real Madrid won <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_La_Liga" title="201920 La Liga">the La Liga title</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Liga_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liga-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201920 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, Madrid were eliminated in the round of 16 by <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> In the second leg at the <a href="/wiki/City_of_Manchester_Stadium" title="City of Manchester Stadium">City of Manchester Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Manchester" title="Manchester">Manchester</a>, Madrid lost the game 21, with Varane being deemed to be at fault for both goals. The mistakes committed by the Frenchman were due to the high pressuring from <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Jesus" title="Gabriel Jesus">Gabriel Jesus</a> which led to Varane losing possession of the ball both times.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> He has since apologised for his mistakes.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth">Youth</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Youth">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Varane was a <a href="/wiki/France_national_youth_football_team" title="France national youth football team">France youth international</a> having earned caps at <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-18_football_team" title="France national under-18 football team">under-18</a> and <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-21_football_team" title="France national under-21 football team">under-21</a> level.
</p><p>Prior to playing for the under-18 team, he was called up to the under-17 team, but did not make an appearance.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_career_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_career-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Varane made his debut with the under-18 team on 24 August 2010 in a <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Exhibition match">friendly match</a> against <a href="/wiki/Denmark_national_under-18_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Denmark national under-18 football team">Denmark</a>. On his debut, he scored the final goal in a 20 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Varane turned down subsequent call-ups to the under-18 team because of his increased participation with the Lens first team and, as a result, missed the <i>Tournoi de Limoges</i> and a tournament in <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-varane_antilles_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varane_antilles-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> On 3 February 2011, he was called up to the under-21 team by coach <a href="/wiki/Erick_Mombaerts" title="Erick Mombaerts">Erick Mombaerts</a> for the first time for a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Slovakia_national_under-21_football_team" title="Slovakia national under-21 football team">Slovakia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Varane described the call up as "a huge surprise".<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> He earned his first under-21 cap and start in the match against Slovakia playing the entire match in a 31 win.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> On 15 November, Varane scored his first under-21 goal in a 20 <a href="/wiki/2013_UEFA_European_Under-21_Football_Championship_qualification" class="mw-redirect" title="2013 UEFA European Under-21 Football Championship qualification">2013 Euro U-21 qualifying</a> win over Slovakia. The victory ensured France qualification to <i>at least</i> the competition's qualifying playoffs.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior">Senior</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Senior">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Raphael_Varane_-_France_v_Armenia.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Raphael_Varane_-_France_v_Armenia.jpg/170px-Raphael_Varane_-_France_v_Armenia.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="226" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Raphael_Varane_-_France_v_Armenia.jpg/255px-Raphael_Varane_-_France_v_Armenia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Raphael_Varane_-_France_v_Armenia.jpg/340px-Raphael_Varane_-_France_v_Armenia.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1620" data-file-height="2152" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Raphael_Varane_-_France_v_Armenia.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Varane playing for <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>In August 2012, Varane was called to the full French national team squad for a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a>, but was an unused substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> He started his first match for France on 22 March 2013 in a qualifier for the World Cup against <a href="/wiki/Georgia_national_football_team" title="Georgia national football team">Georgia</a>, a 31 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> On 13 May 2014, he was included in <a href="/wiki/Didier_Deschamps" title="Didier Deschamps">Didier Deschamps</a>' squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 June 2014, he partnered <a href="/wiki/Mamadou_Sakho" title="Mamadou Sakho">Mamadou Sakho</a> in central defence during <i>Les Bleus'</i> first World Cup fixture  a 30 win over <a href="/wiki/Honduras_national_football_team" title="Honduras national football team">Honduras</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> He was also in the starting line-up for the second group match against <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage" title="2014 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">knockout matches</a> against <a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_football_team" title="Nigeria national football team">Nigeria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a>, as France were eliminated at the quarter-final stage by the Germans 10.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Varane took the blame for allowing <a href="/wiki/Mats_Hummels" title="Mats Hummels">Mats Hummels</a> to hold him off at the critical set-piece which allowed the German defender to head the winning goal.<sup id="cite_ref-FRAURU_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FRAURU-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
In spite of this, Varane was named on the three-man shortlist for the tournament's <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup#Awards" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">Best Young Player</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> On 14 October, Varane became the youngest player to <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> France when he took over from <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Matuidi" title="Blaise Matuidi">Blaise Matuidi</a> at half time in a 30 win over <a href="/wiki/Armenia_national_football_team" title="Armenia national football team">Armenia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> He was then selected as the team's starting captain for a home friendly against <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a> on 18 November, where he scored his first international goal to give <i>Les Bleus</i> a 10 win.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 24 May 2016, he was ruled out of <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a> with a thigh injury, and was replaced by <a href="/wiki/Adil_Rami" title="Adil Rami">Adil Rami</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 17 May 2018, Varane was called up to the 23-man <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_squads" title="2018 FIFA World Cup squads">French squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> He would go on to start in all seven of France's games and play every minute. In the quarterfinal against <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a>, Varane exorcised the memories of the 2014 quarterfinal nightmare as he headed the opening goal in France's 20 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-FRAURU_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FRAURU-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> France later went on to win the competition for the second time in history, and Varane became only the fourth player to be a World Cup champion and Champions League winner in the same year, after <a href="/wiki/Christian_Karembeu" title="Christian Karembeu">Christian Karembeu</a> (in 1998), <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Carlos" title="Roberto Carlos">Roberto Carlos</a> (in 2002), and <a href="/wiki/Sami_Khedira" title="Sami Khedira">Sami Khedira</a> (in 2014). All the players, like Varane, were playing for Real Madrid at the time they won the World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Varane has been described by Lens youth coach <a href="/wiki/Eric_Assadourian" class="mw-redirect" title="Eric Assadourian">Eric Assadourian</a> as a "truly first class player" who is "comfortable on both the tactical and technical level".<sup id="cite_ref-lensois_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lensois-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> On 30 January 2013, the then Real Madrid assistant coach <a href="/wiki/Aitor_Karanka" title="Aitor Karanka">Aitor Karanka</a> talked about Varane in the press conference post-<i>El Clásico</i> of the <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a>, saying, "It's obvious that Varane has a good head on his shoulders and will keep improving."<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Former France defender <a href="/wiki/Frank_Leboeuf" title="Frank Leboeuf">Frank Leboeuf</a> believes that Varane has the potential to be better than Real Madrid legend <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Hierro" title="Fernando Hierro">Fernando Hierro</a>, saying to reporters, "Many compare him to Hierro due to his technique, but on the physical level he is stronger and he is much faster."<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Fernando Hierro and José Mourinho have labelled Varane as one of the best defenders in world football.<sup id="cite_ref-goal1_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal1-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-goal2_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal2-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Varane is married to his long time partner Camille Tytgat<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> and they have a son, named Ruben,<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> and a daughter, Anaïs.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a> called Varane about Real Madrid's interest in signing him in June 2011, Varane asked Zidane to call him back because he was in the middle of revising for his baccalaureate exam.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His sister, Annabelle Varane, was Miss Nord-Pas-de-Calais 2018 and competed in <a href="/wiki/Miss_France_2019" title="Miss France 2019">Miss France 2019</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
